Wanda Realm (REALM) is a series second only to Wanda Ruihua (Reign) and Wanda Vista (Wanda Vista), but its positioning is higher than Jinhua and Meihua.
On the second floor of the hotel, there is a large-scale Pinzhen Chinese restaurant with private rooms of various sizes; on the third floor is the fitness center and swimming pool, which are open from morning to 11 pm, and table tennis facilities cost 40 yuan an hour; hotel weekends And holidays often undertake large-scale wedding banquets.
Some public welfare activities are often held in the hotel lobby on weekends, such as "Earth Hour", during which free small cakes will be provided to guests in the lobby, and free candies will also be provided to children.
I checked in on March 25, 2023. Generally speaking, the hotel meets the five-star standard. The service staff are warm and friendly, and the facilities are complete. The TV in the room can watch foreign channels such as CNN, CNA, HBO, Russia Today, etc. Overall, I am very satisfied. It's just that the parking lot is too small (the underground parking lot can't be used), and you have to wait in line to get a parking space on weekends. You can only use one parking ticket a day; there is no toilet next to the swimming pool. inconvenient.
